      </span><span class="cop-p" data-v-21e3c89c>2009-09-16 09:55:36</span></span> <div class="foot-btn-more" data-v-21e3c89c><!----><!----></div></div></div> <!----> <div id="blogDetail2" class="markdown_views htmledit_views" data-v-0c168368>我使用JEditorPane这个控件&#xff0c;在里面添加HTML的内容&#xff0c;但是HTML文件为中文&#xff0c;就会出现乱码&#xff0c;如下是我的java代码<br /><br />
<br />JEditorPane pane &#61; new JEditorPane();<br />
JEditorPane pane &#61; new JEditorPane();<br />pane.setEditable(false);<br />
pane.setEditable(false);<br />pane.setEditorKit(new HTMLEditorKit());<br />
pane.setEditorKit(new HTMLEditorKit());<br />pane.setContentType(&#34;text/html;charset&#61;UTF-8&#34;);<br />
pane.setContentType(&#34;text/html;charset&#61;UTF-8&#34;);<br />pane.setPage(要显示html的URL);<br />
pane.setPage(要显示html的URL);<br /><br />
<br />我在上面的代码中添加了这句代码pane.setContentType(&#34;text/html;charset&#61;utf-8&#34;);&#xff0c;但是没起作用。<br />
我在上面的代码中添加了这句代码pane.setContentType(&#34;text/html;charset&#61;utf-8&#34;);&#xff0c;但是没起作用。<br />如下是HTML中的内容<br />
如下是HTML中的内容<br /><br />
<br />&lt;html&gt;<br />
&lt;html&gt;<br />&lt;head&gt;<br />
&lt;head&gt;<br />&lt;meta http-equiv&#61;&#34;content-type&#34; content&#61;&#34;text/html;charset&#61;utf-8&#34;&gt;<br />
&lt;meta http-equiv&#61;&#34;content-type&#34; content&#61;&#34;text/html;charset&#61;utf-8&#34;&gt;<br />&lt;/head&gt;<br />
&lt;/head&gt;<br />&lt;body&gt;<br />
&lt;body&gt;<br />测试中文显示<br />
测试中文显示<br />&lt;/body&gt;<br />
&lt;/body&gt;<br />&lt;/html&gt;<br />
&lt;/html&gt;<br /><br />
